<text>Since the new manager has come it has definitely gotten slightly better, at first i loved it, then i realized the tweakers screaming at all hours of the night and the drugged up people walking around like crazy zombies talking to themselves. I lived there for 2 and half years. the pools closed most of the year which sucks. The people there are not all bad but there is a specific park busy body that is a snitch and if your not perfect she will tell on you. Shes old and has a lot of tweaker traffic that goes through her house so who knows what shes about. in 2 and a half years there has been at least 4 park managers. Jack is the newest on and hes great, very helpful and is cleaning up that place so well. the only bad thing is that he doesn't live on site so he doesn't experience the tweakers and so he doesn't do anything about them. HOPEFULLY in time Jack will get that place in better shape. I will say out off all of the parks in Sacramento i have been too this one is the best looking and it has a gate which is very appealing . It is very quiet other then the teenagers during summer roaming around being loud and the tweakers screaming and fighting with themselves and others. no one bothers you there which is nice. I am just glad to be out of there. They need to build a play ground for the kids instead of the basket ball court that rarely gets used. <text>I used to really love this park. Was Colony Mobile Home Park, now is Hometown America Colonial
Estates. They put up an entrance gate then it became 'Estates'.
We had a very friendly community, but our residents got older, died or moved away.
Take a 'short putt' inside and count the amount of empty lots and 'for sale signs' and ask yourself:
WHY ? ? ?
The clubhouse is very well kept...But it seems to not be in much use..
I myself am very disappointed as to the present attitude and concern from the residents and site
management of the health of the community.
I have lived here approx. 20 years. I and my wife as well of most of my neighbors are disabled or are
'Dirt Poor'. It is a struggle to tolerate some of the 'attitude' going on...Perhaps it is ME or the 'sign of the times'...The 'buck($)' seems to be the question and answer, I have neither...</text><pics>None</pics><resp>None<//resp>< GmapID>

I rated a 1 star not because of the service or staff nor the store appearance, the staff was friendly and helpful. I gave the rating because of the return policy.  I purchase a purse for $20.00 on Saturday March 23, 2019 and after I got home I decided that I wanted the other purse I saw that was marked $25.00.  On Sunday March 24, 2019 I took the purse back, and told the clerk that I just wanted to exchange it and pay the difference. I was told that they only exchange/store credit clothing and electronic.  I did not read the receipt return policy, but I just assumed that the purse was included in the clothing.  So I went back on Monday March 25, 2019 and spoke with the manager and was told the same thing.  So I said I still wanted the purse and she said it was $40.00 I said I was here Saturday and it was only $25.00, so no thank you.  She said I can sale it for $30.00 is that okay? I said actually no, she said with your Senior discount it will be $25.50.  I purchased the purse.  My thought is that this is second hand merchandise, and at discount store (Ross, Burlington etc) or Target ,Walmart) New merchandise can be return with or without a receipt.  Also it maybe, but I did not see a large sign that states your return policy.  Will I visit your store again? I am not sure because I usually do not patronize stores with that type of policy that is not clearly visible. People do change their minds as I am sure you have being a consumer.

They have several 50% off days where you can find great deals on furniture, clothing, and other items. Being a thrift store there will be un-organized merchandise but the friendly staff seems to keep most things in order. As a member of the Perris Valley Chamber of Commerce it only solidifies the fact that the work they do is for the community. And, as a director of the chamber and a local attorney I have been able to see the positive impact made by their involvement made in the community.

<Resp>None< /Resp><Name>Heath Sawyer< /Name><Rating>1< /Rating><review>I have never written a review before.
My initial interaction with this service center was good. They seemed knowledgable and very helpful in finding the exact tires that I needed and even ordered them from back east for me. Unfortunately, after purchasing almost a $1000.00 worth of work their customer service went down hill. I was told that the tires would arrive the following Monday (4 days after the initial purchase) and that they would call between 12 and 1pm that day. Monday came and went and I didn't receive a phone call. I called the following day and the person who answered the phone (Atom) was very short with me and seemed as if I was bothering him. He told me that the employee that helped me was wrong on the delivery date and he should have never told me Monday. Atom went on to say, the tires would be in today (Tuesday) between 12-1pm and he would give me a call. No one called! When I called later that day, I was told that in fact Atom was wrong and they where suppose to arrive on Monday. Also,  I was told there was another delay. I would have to wait until Thursday before i would receive the tires. This was a problem, I was set to start a new job in Northern California (+/-12 hours away) that Thursday. If they would have communicated with me back on Monday, I could have made better arrangements. I ended up waiting for the tires and started to leave town when I heard a knocking noise on the front right wheel and turned around and took it back. The tire weight had been mounted wrong. They fixed it, but it took them another hour. At this point I asked for my alignment records. I was told that their printer was down and that they would e-mail it to me. I left and drove north. After waiting a few days for the report I called the service center again. Atom answered the phone, he told me that they couldn't e-mail me the report because only corporate could do that, but he could fax it to me. I waited and no fax. I called back the next day, I was then told they had lost the record.

<time>1602905963628< /time><Rating>4<//Rating>< review>
The beach was great! Exactly how a person would imagine a beach to be; amazingly soothing sand(great exfoliation on the feet), and waves crashing to shore. People surfing and a long peer to walk out on, and even a rescue crew in their little hut. There's plenty of room to do whatever you want,  but there's not a convenient place to park; you have to just get lucky and find one somewhere in the neighborhood. It was alot cleaner than I thought it would be too.<//review>

103209715191462857980< /UserId.>
<user_name>Gene Waring< /user_name>< date>
1601515149819</date>
<rating>5</rating>< review>
Pismo Beach is a wonderful Mediterranean weathered place to visit! There are many hidden beaches that one may enjoy with few if any other people around. There are a variety of wineries to also visit along with some waterfalls that you can swim at and Lake Lopez where you can camp and wakeboard. Kayaking is also very beautiful with some caves that you can go through at Shell Beach. Don't miss the many miles of sand dunes that you can wander through south of Oceano. It is a wonderful place to see a beautiful sunset dropping into the blue jeweled Waters. Having lived here for 30 years I have been fortunate enough to experience all of the area's Many Wonders and would be happy to help others to find some of these secret places! Have you ever heard of the Dunites? They were an incredible people living in the Dunes that had a tremendous effect on the twentieth century yet no one knows about them anymore. Find out more on Instagram: @the_dunites_Utopia.</review>

<rate>5< /rate>< review>
Nice, family friendly beach. Water was ok in December... Warm enough for some people to swim in (if you have a high tolerance for cold water). This beach is also a popular place for surfing, and there is a shop that sells surfer gear close by. The beach is clean, beautiful and long. There are several hotels close by and so many restaurants within walking distance. Parking can be a bit of a hassle the closer you get to the beach front, especially at popular times in the year.< /review>

< Review>
I love Pismo Beach, and I've been coming here since before I could walk. Now with stores, restraunts, and parking being open the feel is like an escape to pre-COVID times. They're currently renovating the whole area surrounding the pier (new bathrooms, a park, slides down to the beach, tables, cornhole, etc.) And their new additions look amazing. They finally reopened parking near Wooly's at the end of Pomeroy which really helps with the flow of traffic. The beach is always clean, and it's a great place to hang out with friends, family, pets, or just go for a peaceful walk on your own. The one drawback is the sheer amount of people who smoke marijuana while walking down the street or on the beach; you literally can not escape the smell if you're anywhere near large groups of people. Otherwise it's great, and I'll definitely be back soon.<//Review>
